\DoxyCodeLine{02648\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02649\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ DESCRIPTION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02650\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02651\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ built\ with\ multiple\ SSL\ backends,\ curl\_global\_sslset()\ allows\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02652\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ choose\ one.\ This\ function\ can\ only\ be\ called\ once,\ and\ it\ must\ be\ called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02653\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ *before*\ curl\_global\_init().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02654\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02655\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ backend\ can\ be\ identified\ by\ the\ id\ (e.g.\ CURLSSLBACKEND\_OPENSSL).\ The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02656\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ backend\ can\ also\ be\ specified\ via\ the\ name\ parameter\ (passing\ -\/1\ as\ id).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02657\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ both\ id\ and\ name\ are\ specified,\ the\ name\ will\ be\ ignored.\ If\ neither\ id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02658\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ nor\ name\ are\ specified,\ the\ function\ will\ fail\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02659\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CURLSSLSET\_UNKNOWN\_BACKEND\ and\ set\ the\ "{}avail"{}\ pointer\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02660\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ NULL-\/terminated\ list\ of\ available\ backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02661\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02662\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Upon\ success,\ the\ function\ returns\ CURLSSLSET\_OK.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02663\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02664\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ the\ specified\ SSL\ backend\ is\ not\ available,\ the\ function\ returns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02665\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ CURLSSLSET\_UNKNOWN\_BACKEND\ and\ sets\ the\ "{}avail"{}\ pointer\ to\ a\ NULL-\/terminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02666\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ list\ of\ available\ SSL\ backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02667\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02668\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ SSL\ backend\ can\ be\ set\ only\ once.\ If\ it\ has\ already\ been\ set,\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02669\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ subsequent\ attempt\ to\ change\ it\ will\ result\ in\ a\ CURLSSLSET\_TOO\_LATE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02670\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02671\ }
